                as for the rest of the sūtrasthāna. (In fact, the transcript of the "1931"
                edition is somewhat mixed between the 1931 and 1938 editions.)</change>

    <text xml:lang="sa-Latn">

        <body>
            <div n="1" type="sthāna">

                <head xml:lang="en">[Sūtrasthāna 1-31]</head>

                <div n="1" type="adhyāya">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.0"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.1">athāto vedotpattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||1|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.2</label>yathovāca bhagavān
                        dhanvantariḥ||2||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.3</label>atha khalu
                        bhagavantam amaravaram ṛṣigaṇaparivṛtam āśramasthaṃ kāśirājaṃ
                        divodāsaṃ dhanvantarim aupadhenava<pc
                            > </pc>vaitaraṇaurabhra<pc> </pc>pauṣkalāvata<pc
                            > </pc>-karavīrya<pc> </pc>gopurarakṣita<pc
                            > </pc>suśruta<pc> </pc>prabhṛtaya ūcuḥ ||3|| <note
                            type="footnote"> karavīra</note>
                    </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.4</label>bhagavan
                        śārīramānasāgantuvyādhibhir vividhavedanābhighātopadrutān sanāthān
                        apy anāthavad viceṣṭamānān vikrośataś ca mānavān abhisamīkṣya
                        manasi naḥ pīḍā bhavati </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.4b"> teṣāṃ sukhaiṣiṇāṃ rogopaśamārtham ātmanaś ca
                        prāṇayātrārthaṃ prajāhitahetor āyurvedaṃ śrotum icchāma
                        ihopadiśyamānaṃ atrāyattam aihikam āmuṣmikaṃ ca śreyaḥ tad
                        bhagavantam upapannāḥ smaḥ śiṣyatveneti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.5</label>tān uvāca bhagavān
                        svāgataṃ vaḥ sarva evāmīmāṃsyā adhyāpyāś ca bhavanto vatsāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.6</label> iha khalv āyurvedaṃ
                        nāmopāṅgam atharvavedasyānutpādyaiva prajāḥ ślokaśatasahasram
                        adhyāyasahasraṃ ca kṛtavān svayambhūḥ tato 'lpāyuṣṭvam
                        alpamedhastvaṃ cālokya narāṇāṃ bhūyo 'ṣṭadhā praṇītavān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.7</label> tad yathā śalyaṃ
                        śālākyaṃ kāyacikitsā bhūtavidyā kaumārabhṛtyaṃ agadatantraṃ
                        rasāyanatantraṃ vājīkaraṇatantram iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.0</label> athāsya
                        pratyaṅgalakṣaṇasamāsaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.1a"> tatra śalyaṃ nāma
                        vividhatṛṇakāṣṭhapāṣāṇapāṃśulohaloṣṭāsthibālanakhapūyāsrāvaduṣṭavraṇāntargarbhaśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ
                        yantraśastrakṣārāgnipraṇidhānavraṇaviniścayārthaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.2</label> śālākyaṃ
                        nāmordhvajatrugatānāṃ śravaṇanayanavadanaghrāṇādisaṃśritānāṃ
                        vyādhīnām upaśamanārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.3</label> kāyacikītsā
                        nāma sarvāṅgasaṃśritānāṃ vyādhīnāṃ
                        jvararaktapittaśoṣonmādāpasmārakuṣṭhamehātisārādīnām
                        upaśamanārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.4</label> bhūtavidyā nāma
                        devāsuragandharvayakṣarakṣaḥpitṛpiśācanāgagrahādyupasṛṣṭacetasāṃ
                        śāntikarmabaloharaṇādigrahopaśamanārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.5</label> kaumārabhṛtyaṃ
                        nāma kumārabharaṇadhātrīkṣīradoṣasaṃśodhanārthaṃ
                        duṣṭastanyagrahasamutthānāṃ ca vyādhīnām upaśamanārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.6</label> agadatantraṃ
                        nāma sarpakīṭalūtāmūśikādidaṣṭaviṣavyañjanārthaṃ
                        vividhaviṣasaṃyogopaśamanārthaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.7</label> rasāyanatantraṃ
                        nāma vayaḥsthāpanam āyurmedhābalakaraṃ rogāpaharaṇasamarthaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.8</label>
                        vājīkaraṇatantraṃ nāmālpaduṣṭakṣīṇaviśuṣkaretasām
                        āpyāyanaprasādopacayajanananimittaṃ praharṣajananārthaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.9</label> evam ayam āyurvedo
                        'ṣṭāṅga upadiśyate atra kasmai kim ucyatām iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.10</label> ta ūcuḥ asmākaṃ
                        sarveṣām eva śalyajñānaṃ mūlaṃ kṛtvopadiśatu bhagavān iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.11</label> sa uvācaivam astv
                        iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.12</label> ta ūcur bhūyo 'pi
                        bhagavantam asmākam ekamatīnāṃ matam abhisamīkṣya suśruto
                        bhagavantaṃ prakṣyati asmai copadiśyamānaṃ vayam apy
                        upadhārayiṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.13</label> sa hovācaivam
                        astv iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.14-16"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.14</label> vatsa suśruta
                        iha khalv āyurvedaprayojanaṃ vyādhyupasṛṣṭānāṃ vyādhiparimokṣaḥ
                        svasthasya rakṣaṇaṃ ca || <label>1931 ed. 1.1.15</label> āyur
                        asmin vidyate 'nena vā+āyur vindatīty āyurvedaḥ || <label>1931 ed.
                            1.1.16</label> tasyāṅgavaram ādyaṃ pratyakṣāgamānumānopamānair
                        aviruddham ucyamānam upadharaya || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.17</label> etad dhy aṅgaṃ
                        prathamaṃ prāg abhighātavraṇasaṃrohāt yajñaśiraḥsandhānāc ca |
                        śrūyate hi yathā rudreṇa yajñasya śiraś chinnam iti tato devā
                        aśvināv abhigamyocuḥ bhagavantau naḥ śreṣṭhatamau yuvāṃ
                        bhaviṣyathaḥ bhavadbhyāṃ yajñasya śiraḥ sandhātavyam iti | tāv
                        ūcatur evam astv iti | atha tayor arthe devā indraṃ yajñabhagena
                        prāsādayan | tābhyāṃ yajñasya śiraḥ saṃhitam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.18</label> aṣṭāsv api
                        cāyurvedatantreṣv etad evādhikam abhimataṃ āmāśu kriyākaraṇād
                        yantraśastrakṣārāgnipraṇidhānāt sarvatantrasāmānyāc ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.19</label> tad idaṃ śāśvataṃ
                        puṇyaṃ svargyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ vṛttikaraṃ ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.20</label> brahmā provāca
                        tataḥ prajāpatir adhijage tasmād aśvinau aśvibhyām indraḥ indrād
                        aḥaṃ mayā tv iha pradeyam arthibhyaḥ prajāhitahetoḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.20x"> bhavati cātra</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.21</label> ahaṃ hi
                        dhanvantarir ādidevo jarārujāmṛtyuharo 'marāṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         śalyāṅgam aṅgair aparair upetaṃ prāpto 'smi gāṃ bhūya ihopadeṣṭum
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.22"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.22</label> asmin śāstre
                        pañcamahābhūtaśarīrisamavāyaḥ puruṣa ity ucyate | tasmin kriyā so
                        'dhiṣṭhānaṃ kasmāt lokasya dvaividhyāt loko hi dvividhaḥ sthāvaro
                        jaṅgamaś ca dvividhātmaka evāgneyaḥ saumyaś ca tadbhūyastvāt
                        pañcātmako vā tatra caturvidho bhūtagrāmaḥ
                        saṃsvedajarāyujāṇḍajodbhijjasaṃjñaḥ tatra puruṣaḥ pradhānaṃ
                        tasyopakaraṇam anyat tasmāt puruṣo 'dhiṣṭhānam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.23"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.23</label> tadduḥkhasaṃyogā
                        vyādhaya ucyante || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.24"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.24</label> te caturvidhāḥ
                        āgantavaḥ śārīrāḥ mānasāḥ svābhāvikāś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.1</label> teṣām
                        āgantavo 'bhighātanimittāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.2</label> śārīrās tv
                        annapānamūlā vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātavaiṣamyanimittāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.3</label> mānasās tu
                        krodhaśokabhayaharṣaviṣāderṣyābhyasūyādainyamātsaryakāmalobhaprabhṛtaya
                        icchādveṣabhedair bhavanti || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.4</label> svābhāvikās
                        tu kṣutpipāsājarāmṛtyunidrāprakṛtayaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.26"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.26</label> ta ete
                        manaḥśarīrādhiṣṭhānāḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.27"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.27</label> teṣāṃ
                        saṃśodhanasaṃśamanāhārācārāḥ samyak prayuktā nigrahahetavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.28"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.28</label> prāṇināṃ punar
                        mūlam āhāro balavarṇaujasāṃ ca sa ṣaṭsu raseṣv āyattaḥ rasāḥ punar
                        dravyāśrayāḥ dravyāṇi punar oṣadhayaḥ | tās tu dvividhāḥ sthāvarā
                        jaṅgamāś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.29"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.29</label> tāsāṃ sthāvarāś
                        caturvidhāḥ vanaspatayo vṛkṣā vīrudha oṣadhaya iti | tāsu apuṣpāḥ
                        phalavanto vanaspatayaḥ puṣpaphalavanto vṛkṣāḥ pratānavatyaḥ
                        stambinyaś ca vīrudhaḥ phalapākaniṣṭhā oṣadhaya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.30"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.30</label> jaṅgamāḥ khalv
                        api caturvidhāḥ jarāyujāṇḍajasvedajodbhijjāḥ | tatra
                        paśumanuṣyavyālādayo jarāyujāḥ khagasarpasarīsṛpaprabhṛtayo
                        'ṇḍajāḥ kṛmikīṭapipīlikāprabhṛtayaḥ svedajāḥ
                        indragopamaṇḍūkaprabhṛtaya udbhijjāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.31"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.31</label> tatra
                        sthāvarebhyas tvakpatrapuṣpaphalamūlakandaniryāsasvarasādayaḥ
                        prayojanavantaḥ jaṅgamebhyaś carmanakharomarudhirādayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.32"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.32</label> pārthivāḥ
                        suvarṇarajatamaṇimuktāmanaḥśilāmṛtkapālādayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.33"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.33</label> kālakṛtāḥ
                        pravātanivātātapacchāyājyotsnātamaḥśītoṣṇavarṣāhorātrapakṣamāsartvayanādayaḥ
                        saṃvatsaraviśeṣāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.34"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.34</label> ta ete svabhāvata
                        eva doṣāṇāṃ sañcayaprakopapraśamapratīkārahetavaḥ prayojanavantaś
                        ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.35"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.35</label> bhavanti cātra
                        ślokāḥ </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.35x"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.35</label> śārīrāṇāṃ
                        vikārāṇām eṣa vargaś caturvidhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakope praśame caiva hetur uktaś cikitsakaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.36"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.36</label> āgantavas tu ye
                        rogās te dvidhā nipatanti hi |
                        <caesura/>
                         manasy anye śarīre 'nye teṣāṃ tu dvividhā kriyā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.37"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.37</label> śarīrapatitānāṃ
                        tu śārīravad upakramaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mānasānāṃ tu śabdādir iṣṭo vargaḥ sukhāvahaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.38"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.38</label> evam etat puruṣo
                        vyādhir auṣadhaṃ kriyā kāla iti catuṣṭayaṃ samāsena vyākhyātam |
                        tatra puruṣagrahaṇāt tatsaṃbhavadravyasamūho bhūtādir uktas
                        tadaṅgapratyaṅgavikalpāś ca tvaṅmāṃsāsthisirāsnāyuprabhṛtayaḥ
                        vyādhigrahaṇād vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātavaiṣamyanimittāḥ sarva
                        eva vyādhayo vyākhyātāḥ oṣadhagrahaṇād
                        dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākānām ādeśaḥ kriyāgrahaṇāc chedyādīni
                        snehādīni ca karmāṇi vyākhyātāni kālagrahaṇāt sarvakriyākālānām
                        ādeśaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.39x"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.39</label> bhavati cātra | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.39"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.39</label> bījaṃ
                        cikitsitasyaitat samāsena prakīrtitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         saviṃśam adhyāyaśatam asya vyākhyā bhaviṣyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.40"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.40</label> tac ca saviṃśam
                        adhyāyaśataṃ pañcasu sthāneṣu sūtranidānaśārīracikitsitakalpeṣv
                        arthavaśāt saṃvibhajya uttare tantre śeṣān arthān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.41x"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.41</label>
                    </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.41"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.41</label>bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         svayambhuvā proktam idaṃ sanātanaṃ
                        <caesura/>
                         paṭhed dhi yaḥ kāśipatiprakāśitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa puṇyakarmā bhuvi pūjito nṛpair
                        <caesura/>
                         asukṣaye śakrasalokatāṃ vrajet || </l>




                    <p xml:id="SS.1.1">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne vedotpattir nāma
                        prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                </div>


                <div n="2" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ|]</head>

                    <p xml:id="SS.1.2.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.1</label> athātaḥ
                        śiṣyopanayanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </p>

                    <p xml:id="SS.1.2.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                        dhanvantariḥ || </p>

                    <p xml:id="SS.1.2.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.3</label>
                        brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyānām anyatamam anvaya<pc
                            > </pc>vayaḥ<pc/>śīla<pc> </pc>śaurya<pc
                            > </pc>śaucācāra<pc> </pc>vinaya<pc> </pc>śakti<pc
                            > </pc>bala<pc> </pc>medhā<pc> </pc>dhṛti<pc
                            > </pc>smṛti<pc> </pc>mati<pc> </pc>pratipattiyuktaṃ
                            tanu<pc> </pc>jihvauṣṭha<pc> </pc>dantāgram ṛjuvaktrākṣināsaṃ
                        prasannacittavākceṣṭaṃ kleśasahaṃ ca bhiṣak śiṣyam upanayet ato
                        viparītaguṇaṃ nopanayet || </p>

                    <p xml:id="SS.1.2.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.4</label> upanayanīyaṃ tu
                        brāhmaṇaṃ praśasteṣu tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu praśastāyāṃ diśi
                        śucau same deśe caturhastaṃ caturasraṃ sthaṇḍilam upalipya
                        gomayena darbhaiḥ saṃstīrya puṣpair lājabhaktai ratnaiś ca devatāḥ
                        pūjayitvā viprān bhiṣajaś ca tatrollikhyābhyukṣya ca dakṣiṇato
                        brahmāṇaṃ sthāpayitvā'gnim upasamādhāya
                        khadirapalāśadevadārubilvānāṃ samidbhiś caturṇāṃ vā kṣīravṛkṣāṇāṃ
                        (? nyagrodhodumbarāśvatthamadhūkānāṃ ) dadhimadhughṛtāktābhir
                        dārvīhaumikena vidhinā sruveṇājyāhutīr juhuyāt sapraṇavābhir
                        mahāvyahṛtibhiḥ tataḥ pratidaivatamṛṣīṃś ca svāhākāraṃ kuryāt
                        śiṣyam api kārayet || </p>

                    <p xml:id="SS.1.2.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.5</label> brāhmaṇas trayāṇāṃ
                        varṇānām upanayanaṃ kartum arhati rājanyo dvayasya vaiśyo
                        vaiśyasyaiveti śūdram api kulaguṇasaṃpannaṃ mantravarjam
                        anupanītam adhyāpayed ity eke || </p>

                    <p xml:id="SS.1.2.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.6</label> tato 'gniṃ triḥ
                        pariṇīyāgnisākṣikaṃ śiṣyaṃ brūyāt
                        kāmakrodhalobhamohamānāhaṇkārerṣyāpāruṣyapaiśunyānṛtālasyāyaśasyāni
                        hitvā nīcanakharomṇā śucinā kaṣāyavāsasā
                        satyavratabrahmacaryābhivādanatatpareṇā'vaśyaṃ bhavitavyaṃ
                        madanumatasthānagamanaśayanāsanabhojanādhyayanapareṇa bhūtvā
                        matpriyahiteṣu vartitavyaṃ ato 'nyathā te vartamānasyādharmo
                        bhavati aphalā ca vidyā na ca prākāśyaṃ prāpnoti || </p>

                    <p xml:id="SS.1.2.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.7</label> ahaṃ vā tvayi
                        samyagvartamāne yady anyathādarśī syām enobhāg bhaveyam
                        aphalavidyaś ca || </p>

                    <p xml:id="SS.1.2.7.a"/>

                    <p xml:id="SS.1.2.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.8</label>
                        dvijagurudaridramitrapravrajitopanatasādhvanāthābhyupagatānāṃ
                        cātmabāndhavānām iva svabhaiṣajaiḥ pratikartavyam evaṃ sādhu
                        bhavati vyādhaśākunikapatitapāpakāriṇāṃ ca na pratikartavyaṃ evaṃ
                        vidyā prakāśate mitra<pc> </pc>yaśo<pc> </pc>dharmārtha<pc
                        > </pc>kāmāṃś ca prāpnoti || </p>

                    <p xml:id="SS.1.2.9X"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.9x</label> bhavataś cātra | </p>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.9</label> kṛṣṇe 'ṣṭamī
                        tannidhane 'hanī dve
                        <caesura/>
                         śukle tathā 'py evam ahar dvisandhyam |
                        <caesura/>
                         akālavidyutstanayitnughoṣe
                        <caesura/>
                         svatantrarāṣṭrakṣitipavyathāsu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.10</label>
                        śmaśānayānādyatanāhaveṣu
                        <caesura/>
                         mahotsavautpātikadarśaneṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         nādhyeyam anyeṣu ca yeṣu vaprā
                        <caesura/>
                         nādhīyate nāśucinā ca nityam || </l>

                    <p xml:id="SS1.2.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        śiṣyopanayanīyo nāma dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                </div>

                <div n="6" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>śaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.1</label> athāta ṛtucaryam
                        adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                        dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.3</label> kālo hi nāma
                        bhagavān svayambhur anādimadhyanidhano 'tra rasavyāpatsampattī
                        jīvitamaraṇe ca manuṣyāṇām āyatte | sa sūkṣmām api kalāṃ na līyata
                        iti kālaḥ saṃkalayati kālayati vā bhūtānīti kālaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.4</label> tasya
                        saṃvatsarātmano bhagavān ādityo gativiśeṣeṇa
                        nimeṣakāṣṭhākalāmuhūrtāhorātrapakṣamāsartvayanasaṃvatsarayugapravibhāgaṃ
                        karoti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.5</label> tatra
                        laghvakṣaroccāraṇamātro 'kṣinimeṣaḥ pañcadaśā'kṣinimeṣāḥ kāṣṭhā
                        triṃśatkāṣṭhāḥ kalā viṃśatikalo muhūrtaḥ kalādaśabhāgaś ca
                        triṃśanmuhūrtam ahorātraṃ pañcadaśāhorātrāṇi pakṣaḥ sa ca
                        dvividhaḥ śuklaḥ kṛṣṇaś ca tau māsaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.6</label> tatra māghādayo
                        dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ dvimāsikam ṛtuṃ kṛtva ṣaḍṛtavo bhavanti
                        te śiśiravasantagrīṣmavarṣāśaraddhemantāḥ teṣaṃ tapastapsyau
                        śiśiraḥ madhumādhavau vasantaḥ śuciśukrau grīṣmaḥ nabhonabhasyau
                        varśāḥ iṣorjau śarat sahaḥsahasyau hemanta iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.7</label> ta ete
                        śītoṣṇavarṣalakṣaṇāś candrād ity ayoḥ kālavibhāgakaratvād ayane
                        dve bhavato dakṣiṇam uttaraṃ ca | tayor dakṣiṇaṃ
                        varṣāśaraddhemantāḥ teṣu bhagavān āpyāyate somaḥ
                        amlalavaṇamadhurāś ca rasā balavanto bhavanti uttarottaraṃ ca
                        sarvaprāṇināṃ balam abhivardhate | uttaraṃ ca śiśiravasantagrīṣmāḥ
                        teṣu bhagavān āpyāyate 'rkaḥ tiktakaṣāyakaṭukāś ca rasā balavanto
                        bhavanti uttarottaraṃ ca sarvaprāṇināṃ balam apahīyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.8</label> bhavati cātra | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.8ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.8ab</label> śītāṃśuḥ
                        kledayaty urvīṃ vivasvān śoṣayaty api | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.8cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.8cd</label> tāv ubhāv api
                        saṃśritya vāyuḥ pālayati prajāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.9</label> atha khalv ayane
                        dve yugapat saṃvatsaro bhavati te tu pañca yugam iti saṃjñāṃ
                        labhante sa eṣa nimeṣādir yugaparyantaḥ kālaś cakravat
                        parivartamānaḥ kālacakram ucyata ity eke || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.10</label> iha tu
                        varṣāśaraddhemantavasantagrīṣmaprāvṛṣaḥ ṣaḍṛtavo bhavanti
                        doṣopacayaprakopopaśamanimittaṃ te tu bhādrapadādyena dvimāsikena
                        vyākhyātāḥ tad yathā bhādrapadāśvayujau varṣāḥ kārtikamārgaśīrṣau
                        śarat pauṣamāghau hemantaḥ phālgunacaitrau vasantaḥ
                        vaiśākhajyeṣṭhau grīṣmaḥ āṣāḍhaśrāvaṇau prāvṛḍ iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.11</label> tatra varṣāsv
                        oṣadhayas taruṇyo 'lpavīryā āpaś cāprasannāḥ kṣitimalaprāyāḥ tā
                        upayujyamānā nabhasi meghāvatate jalapraklinnāyāṃ bhūmau
                        klinnadehānāṃ prāṇināṃ śītavātaviṣṭambhitāgnīnāṃ vidahyante
                        vidāhāt pittasaṃcayam āpādayanti sa saṃcayaḥ śaradi praviralameghe
                        viyaty upaśuṣyati paṅke 'rkakiraṇapravilāyitaḥ paittikān vyādhīn
                        janayati | tā evauṣadhayaḥ kālapariṇāmāt pariṇatavīryā balavatyo
                        hemante bhavanty āpaś ca prasannāḥ snigdhā atyarthaṃ gurvyaś ca tā
                        upayujyamānā mandakiraṇatvād bhānoḥ
                        satuṣārapavanopastambhitadehānāṃ dehinām avidagdhāḥ snehāc
                        chaityād gauravād upalepāc ca śleṣmasaṃcayam āpādayanti sa saṃcayo
                        vasante 'rkraśmipravilāyita īṣatstabdhadehānāṃ dehināṃ ślaiṣmikān
                        vyādhīn janayati | tā evauṣadhayo nidāghe niḥsārā rūkṣā atimātraṃ
                        laghvyo bhavanty āpaś ca tā upayujyamānāḥ
                        sūryapratāpopaśoṣitadehānāṃ dehināṃ raukṣyāl laghutvād vaiśadyāc
                        ca vāyoḥ saṃcayam āpādyanti sa saṃcayaḥ prāvṛṣi cātyarthaṃ
                        jalopaklinnāyāṃ bhūmau klinnadehānāṃ prāṇināṃ śītavātavarṣerito
                        vātikān vyādhīn janayati | evam eṣa doṣāṇāṃ saṃcayaprakopahetur
                        uktaḥ ||</l>

                    <head>saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.1</label> athāto yantravidhim
                        adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                        dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.3</label> yantraśatam
                        ekottaraṃ atra hastam eva pradhānatamaṃ yantrāṇām avagaccha (?.kiṃ
                        kāraṇaṃ yasmād dhastād ṛte yantrāṇām apravṛttir eva )
                        tadadhīnatvād yantrakarmaṇām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.4</label> tatra
                        manaḥśarīrābādhakarāṇi śalyāni teṣām āharaṇopāyo yantrāṇi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.5</label> tāni ṣaṭprakārāṇi
                        tad yathā svastikayantrāṇi saṃdaṃśayantrāṇi tālayantrāṇi
                        nāḍīyantrāṇi śalākāyantrāṇi upayantrāṇi ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.6</label> tatra caturviṃśatiḥ
                        svastikayantrāṇi dve saṃdaṃśayantre dve eva tālayantre
                        viṃśatirnāḍyaḥ aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ śalākāḥ panñcaviṃśatirupayantrāṇi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.7</label> tāni prāyaśo
                        lauhāni bhavanti tatpratirūpakāṇi vā tadalābhe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.8</label> tatra
                        nānāprakārāṇāṃ vyālānāṃ mṛgapakṣiṇāṃ mukhair mukhāni yantrāṇāṃ
                        prāyaśaḥ sadṛśāni tasmāt
                        tatsārūpyādāgamādupadeśādanyayantradarśanādyuktitaś ca kārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.9ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.9ab</label> samāhitāni
                        yantrāṇi kharaślakṣṇamukhāni ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.9cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.9cd</label> sudṛḍhāni
                        surūpāṇi sugrahāṇi ca kārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.10</label> tatra
                        svastikayantrāṇi aṣṭādaśāṅgulapramāṇāni
                        siṃhavyāghravṛkatarakṣvṛkṣadvīpimārjāraśṛgālamṛgair
                        ivārukakākakaṅkakuraracāsabhāsaśaśaghātyulūkacilliśyenagṛdhrakrauñcabhṛṅgarājāñjalikarṇāvabhañjananandi(ā.ndī)mukhamukhāni
                        masūrākṛtibhiḥ kīlair avabaddhāni mūle 'ṅkuśavadāvṛttavāraṅgāṇi
                        asthividaṣṭaśalyoddharaṇārtham upadiśyante || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.11</label> sanigraho
                        'nigrahaś ca saṃdaṃśau ṣoḍaśāṅgulau bhvataḥ tau
                        svaṅnāṃsasirāsnāyugataśalyoddharaṇārtham upadiśyete || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.12</label> tālayantre
                        dvādaśāṅgule matsyatālavadekatāladvitālake
                        karṇanāsānāḍīśalyānāmāharaṇārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.13</label> nāḍīyantrāṇi
                        apyanekaprakārāṇi anekaprayojanāni ekatomukhānyubhayatomukhāni ca
                        tāni srotogataśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ rogadarśanārthaṃ ācūṣaṇārthaṃ
                        kriyāsaukaryārthaṃ ceti tāni srotodvārapariṇāhāni
                        yathāyogadīrghāṇi ca | tatra
                        bhagandarārśovraṇabastyuttarabastimūtravṛddhidakodaradhūmaniruddhaprakaśasanniruddhagudayantrāṇy
                        alābūśṛṅgayantrāṇi coprariṣṭād vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.14</label> śalākāyantrāṇy
                        api nānāprakārāṇi nānāprayojanāni yathāyogapariṇāhadīrghāṇi ca
                        teṣāṃ gaṇḍūpadasarpaphaṇaśarapuṅkhabaḍiśamukhe dve dve
                        eṣaṇavyūhanacālanāharaṇārtham upadiśyete masūradalamātramukhe dve
                        kiṃcidānatāgre srotogataśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ ṣaṭ kārpāsakṛtoṣṇīṣāṇi
                        pramārjanakriyāsu trīṇi darvyākṛtīni khallamukhāni
                        kṣārauṣadhapraṇidhānārthaṃ trīṇyanyāni jāmbavavadanāni
                        trīṇyaṅkuśavadanāni ṣaḍevāgnikarmasvabhipretāni
                        nāsārbudaharaṇārthamekaṃ kolāsthidalamātramukhaṃ khallatīkṣṇoṣṭhaṃ
                        añjanārthamekaṃ kalāyaparimaṇḍalamubhuyato mukulāgraṃ
                        mūtramārgaviśodhanārthamekaṃ
                        mālatīpuṣpavṛntāgrapramāṇaparimaṇḍalam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.15</label>
                        upayantrāṇyapi-rajjuveṇikāpaṭṭacarmāntavalkalalatāvastrāṣṭhīlāśmamudgarapāṇipādatalāṅgulijihvādantanakhamukhabālāśvakaṭakaśākhāṣṭhīvanapravāhaṇaharṣāyaskāntamayāni
                        kṣārāgnibheṣajāni ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.16ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.16ab</label> etāni dehe
                        sarvasmin dehasyāvayave tathā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.16cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.16cd</label> saṃdhau
                        koṣṭhe dhamanyāṃ ca yathāyogaṃ prayojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.17</label> yantrakarmāṇi tu
                        nirghātanapūraṇabandhanavyūhanavartanacālanavivartanavivaraṇapīḍanamārgaviśodhanavikarṣaṇāharaṇāñchanonnamanavinamanabhañjanonmathanācūṣaṇaiṣaṇadāraṇarjūkaraṇaprakṣālanapradhamanapramārjanāni
                        caturviṃśatiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.18ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.18ab</label> svabuddhyā
                        cāpi vibhajedyantrakarmāṇi buddhimān | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.18cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.18cd</label>
                        asaṃkhyeyavikalpatvāc chalyānām iti niścayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.19</label> tatra atisthūlaṃ
                        asāraṃ atidīrghaṃ atihrasvaṃ agrāhi viṣamagrāhi vakraṃ śithilaṃ
                        atyunnataṃ mṛdukīlaṃ mṛdumukhaṃ mṛdupāśam iti dvādaśa yantradoṣāḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.20ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.20ab</label> etair doṣair
                        vinirmuktaṃ yantramaṣṭādaśāṅgulam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.20cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.20cd</label> praśastaṃ
                        bhiṣajā jñeyaṃ taddhi karmasu yojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.21ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.21ab</label> dṛśyaṃ
                        siṃhamukhādyais tu gūḍhaṃ kaṅkamukhādibhiḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.21cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.21cd</label> nirharet tu
                        śanaiḥ śalyaṃ śa(ā.śā)strayuktivyapekṣayā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.22ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.22ab</label>
                        ni(ā.vi)vartate sādhvavagāhate ca śalyaṃ nigṛhyoddharate ca yasmāt
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.22cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.22cd</label> yantreṣv ataḥ
                        kaṅkamukhaṃ pradhānaṃ sthāneṣu sarveṣv adhi(ā.vi)kāri caiva || </l>
                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne yantravidhirnāma
                        saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>

                <div n="8" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>aṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.1</label> athātaḥ
                        śastrāvacāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                        dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.3</label> viṃśatiḥ śāstrāṇi
                        tad yathā
                        maṇḍalāgrakarapatravṛddhipatranakhaśastramudrikotpalapatrakārdhadhārasūcīkuśapatrāṭīmukhaśarārimaukhāntarmukhatrikūrcakakuṭhārikāvrīhimukhārāvetasapatrakabaḍiśadantaśaṅkveṣaṇya
                        iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.4</label> tatra
                        maṇḍalāgrakarapatre syātāṃ chedane lekhane ca
                        vṛddhipatranakhaśastramudrikotpalapatrakārdhadhārāṇi chedane
                        bhedane ca sūcīkuśapatrāṭīmukhaśarārimukhāntarmukhatrikūrcakāni
                        visrāvaṇe kuṭhārikāvrīhimukhārāvetasapatrakāṇi vyadhane sūcī ca
                        baḍiśaṃ dantaśaṅkuś cāharaṇe eṣaṇyeṣaṇe ānulobhye ca sūcyaḥ sīvane
                        ity aṣṭavidhe karmaṇyupayogaḥ śastrāṇāṃ vyākkhyātaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.5</label> teṣamatha
                        yathāyogaṃ grahaṇasamāsopāyaḥ karmasuvakṣyate tatra vṛddhipatraṃ
                        vṛntaphalasādhāraṇe bhāge gṛhṇīyādbhedanānyevaṃ sarvāṇi
                        vṛddhipatraṃ maṇḍalāgraṃ ca kiṃciduttānena pāṇinā lekhane bahuśo
                        'vacāryaṃ vṛntāgre visrāvaṇāni viśeṣeṇa tu
                        bālavṛddhasukumārabhīrunārīṇāṃ rājñāṃ rājaputrāṇāṃ ca trikūrcakena
                        visrāvayet talapracchāditavṛntamaṅguṣṭhapradeśinībhyāṃ vrīhimukhaṃ
                        kuṭhārikāṃ
                        vāmahastanyastāmitarahastamadhyamāṅgulyā'ṅguṣṭhaviṣṭabdhayā'bhihanyāt
                        ārākarapatraiṣaṇyo mūle śeṣāṇi tu yathāyogaṃ kṛhṇīyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.5a"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.6</label> teṣāṃ nāmabhir
                        evākṛtayaḥ prāyeṇa vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.7</label> tatra
                        nakhaśastraiṣaṇyāvaṣṭāṅgule sūcyo vakṣyante (?
                        pradeśinyagraparvapradeśapramāṇā mudrikā daśāṅgulā śarārimukhī sā
                        ca kartarīti kathyate |) śeṣāṇi tu ṣaḍaṅgulāni || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.8</label> tāni sugrahāṇi
                        sulohāni sudhārāṇi surūpāṇi susamāhitamukhāgrāṇi akarālāni ceti
                        śastrasaṃpat || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.9</label> tatra vakraṃ
                        kuṇṭhaṃ khaṇḍaṃ kharadhāraṃ atisthūlaṃ atitucchaṃ atidīrghaṃ
                        atihrasvaṃ ity aṣṭau śastradoṣāḥ | ato viparītaguṇam ādadīta
                        anyatra karapatrāt taddhi kharadhāramasthicchedanārtham// </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.10</label> tatra dhārā
                        bhedanānāṃ māsūrī lekhanānām ardhamāsūrī vyadhanānāṃ visrāvaṇānāṃ
                        ca kaiśikī chedanānām ardhakaiśikīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.11</label> baḍiśaṃ
                        dantaśaṅkuś cānatāgre | tīkṣṇakaṇṭakaprathamayavapatramukhyeṣaṇī
                        (? gaṇḍūpadākāramukhī ca ) || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.12</label> teṣāṃ pāyanā
                        trividhā kśārodakataileṣu | tatra kṣārapāyitaṃ
                        śaraśalyāsthicchedaneṣu udakapāyitaṃ māṃsacchedanabhedanapāṭaneṣu
                        tailapāyitaṃ sirāvyadhanasnāyucchedaneṣu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.13</label> teṣāṃ niśānārthaṃ
                        ślakṣṇaśilā māṣavarṇā dhārāsaṃsthāpanārthaṃ śālmalīphalakam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.14</label> bhavati cātra | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.14ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.14ab</label> yadā
                        suniśitaṃ śastraṃ romacchedi susaṃsthitam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.14cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.14cd</label> sugṛhītaṃ
                        pramāṇena tadā karmasu yojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.15</label> anuśastrāṇi tu
                        tvaksārasphaṭikakācakuruvindajalaukognikṣāranakhagojīśephālikāśākapatrakarīrabālāṅgulaya
                        iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.16ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.16ab</label> śiṣūnāṃ
                        śastrabhīrūṇāṃ śastrābhāve ca yojayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.16cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.16cd</label>
                        tvaksārādicaturvargaṃ chedye ca buddhimān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.17ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.17ab</label>
                        āhāryacchedyabhedyeṣu nakhaṃ śakyeṣu yojayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.17cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.17cd</label> vidhiḥ
                        pravakṣyate paścāt kṣāravahnijalaukasām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.18ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.18ab</label> ye syur
                        mukhagatā rogā netravartmagatāś ca ye | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.18cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.18cd</label>
                        gojīśephālikāśākapatrair visrāvayet tu tān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.19ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.19ab</label>
                        eṣyeṣveṣaṇyalābhe tu bālāṅgulyaṅkurā hitāḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.19cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.19cd</label> śastrāṇy
                        etāni matimān śuddhaśaikyāyasāni tu | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.19ef"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.19ef</label> kārayet
                        karaṇaprāptaṃ karmāraṃ karmakovidam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.20ab</label> prayogajñasya
                        vaidyasya siddhir bhavati nity aśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.20cd</label> tasmāt paricayaṃ kuryāc
                        chastrāṇāṃ grahaṇe sadā || </l>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne śastrāvacāraṇīyo
                        nāmāṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>

                <div n="9" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>navamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.1</label> athāto
                        yogyāsūtrīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                        dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.3</label>
                        adhigatasarvaśāstrārtham api śiṣyaṃ yogyāṃ kārayet | snehādiṣu
                        chedyādīṣu ca karmapatham upadiśet | subahuśruto 'pyakṛtayogyaḥ
                        karmasvayogyo bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.4</label> tatra
                        puṣpaphalālābūkālindakatrapusai(ā.so)rvārukarkārukaprabhṛtiṣu
                        chedyaviśeṣān darśayet utkartanaparikartanāni copadiśet
                        dṛtibastiprasevakaprabhṛtiṣūdakapaṅkapūrṇeṣu bhedyayogyāṃ saromṇi
                        carmaṇyātate lekhyasya mṛtapaśusirāsūtpalanāleṣu ca vedhyasya
                        ghuṇopahatakāṣṭhaveṇunalanālīśuṣkālābūmukheṣveṣyasya
                        panasabimbībilvaphalamajjamṛtapaśudanteṣvāhāryasya
                        madhūcchiṣṭopalipte śālmalīphalake visrāvyasya
                        sūkṣmaghanavastrāntayor mṛducarmāntayoś ca sīvyasya
                        pustamayapuruśāṅgapratyaṅgaviśeṣeṣu bandhanayogyāṃ
                        mṛducarmamāṃsapeśīṣūtpalanāleṣu ca karṇasandhibandhayogyāṃ mṛduṣu
                        māṃsakhaṇḍeṣv agnikṣārayogyāṃ
                        udakapūṇaghaṭapārśvasrotasyalābūmukhādiṣu ca
                        netrapraṇidhānabastivraṇabastipīḍanayogyām iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.5</label> bhavataś cātra | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.5ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.5ab</label> evam ādiṣu
                        medhāvī yogyārheṣu yathāvidhi | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.5cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.5cd</label> dravyeṣu yogyāṃ
                        kurvāṇo na pramuhyati karmasu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.6ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.6ab</label> tasmāt
                        kauśalamanvicchan śastrakṣārāgnikarmasu | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.6cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.6cd</label> yasya yatreha
                        sādharmyaṃ tatra yogyāṃ samācaret || </l>
                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne yogyāsūtrīyo nāma
                        navamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                </div>
                <div n="10" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.1</label> athāto
                        viśikhānupraveśanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.2</label> yathovāca
                        bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.3</label>
                        adhigatatantreṇopāsitatantrārthena dṛṣṭakarmaṇā kṛtayogyena
                        śāstraṃ nigadatā rājānujñātena nīcanakharomṇā ṣucinā
                        śuklavastraparihitena chatravatā daṇḍahastena
                        sopānatkenānuddhataveśena sumanasā kalyāṇābhivyāhāreṇākuhakena
                        bandhubhūtena bhūtānāṃ susahāyavatā vaidyena niśikhā'nupraveṣṭavyā
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.4</label> tato
                        dūtanimittaśakunamaṅgalānulomyenāturagṛhamabhigamya upaviśya
                        āturamabhipaśyet spṛśet pṛcchec ca tribhir etair vijñānopāyai
                        rogāḥ prāyaśo veditavyā ity eke tat tu na samyak ṣaḍvidho hi
                        rogāṇāṃ vijñānopāyaḥ tad yathā pañcabhiḥ śrotrādibhiḥ praśnena
                        ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.5</label> tatra
                        śrotrendriyavijñeyā viśeṣā rogeṣu vraṇāsrāvanijñānīyādiṣu
                        vakṣyante tatra saphenaṃ raktam īrayann anilaḥ saśabdo nirgacchati
                        ity evam ādayaḥ sparśanendriyavijñeyāḥ
                        śītoṣṇaślakṣṇakarkaśamṛdukaṭhinatvād ayaḥ sparśaviśeṣā
                        jvaraśophādeṣu cakṣurindriyavijñeyāḥ
                        śarīropacayāpacayāyurlakṣaṇabalavarṇavikārādayaḥ
                        rasanendriyavijñeyāḥ pramehādiṣu rasaviśeṣāḥ ghrāṇendriyavijñeyā
                        ariṣṭaliṅgādiṣu vraṇānāmavraṇānāṃ ca gandhaviśeṣāḥ praśnena ca
                        vijānīyāddeśaṃ kālaṃ jātiṃ sātmyamātaṅkasamutpattiṃ
                        vedanāsamucchrāyaṃ balamantaragniṃ vātamūtrapurīṣāṇāṃ
                        pravṛttyapravṛttī kālaprakarṣādīṃś ca viśeṣān | ātmasadṛśeṣu
                        vijñānābhyupāyeṣu tatsthānīyair jānīyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.6</label> bhavati cātra | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.6ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.6ab</label> mithyādṛṣṭā
                        vikārā hi durākhyātās tathaiva ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.6cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.6cd</label> tathā
                        duṣparimṛṣṭāś ca mohayeyuś cikitsakam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.6ef"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.7</label> yāpayet asādhyān
                        nopakramet parisaṃvatsarotthitāṃś ca vikārān prāyaśo varjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.8</label> tatra sādhyā api
                        vyādhayaḥ prāyeṇaiṣāṃ duścikitsyatamā bhavanti | tad yathā
                        śrotriyanṛpatistrībālavṛddhabhīrurājasevakakitavadrubalavaidyavidagdhavyādhigopakadaridrakṛpaṇakrodhanānāmanātmavatāmanāthānāṃ
                        ca evaṃ nirūpya cikitsāṃ kurvan dharmārthakāmayaśāṃsi prāpnoti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.9</label> bhavati cātra | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.9ab</label> strībhiḥ
                        sahāsyāṃ saṃvāsaṃ parihāsaṃ ca varjayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.9cd</label> dattaṃ ca
                        tābhyo nādeyam annād anyad bhiṣagvaraiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9ef"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9ef1"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9gh"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9gh1"/>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        viśikhānupraveśanīyo nāma daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>





                </div>



                <div n="11" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>ekādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.1</label> athātaḥ
                        kṣārapākavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.2</label> yathovāca

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.5</label>

                        saumyasyāpi sato dahanapacanadāraṇādiśaktiraviruddhā sa khalv

                        saptasu ca mukharogeṣūpajihvādhijihvopakuśadantavaidarbheṣu tisṛṣu

                        cetarakṣāravad dagdhvā parisrāvayet tasya vistaro 'nyatra || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.11</label> athetaras
                        trividho mṛdurmadhyastīkṣṇaś ca | taṃ cikīrṣuḥ śaradi girisānujaṃ
                        śucir upoṣya praśaste 'hani praśastadeśajātam anupahataṃ
                        madhyamavayasaṃ mahāntamasitamuṣkakamadhivāsyāparedyuḥ pāṭayitvā
                        svaṇḍaśaḥ prakalpyāvapāṭya nirvāte deśe nicitiṃ kṛtvā
                        sudhāśarkarāś ca prakṣipya nilanālair ādīpayet | athopaśānte 'gnau
                        tadbhasma pṛthaggṛhṇīyādbhasmaśarkarāś ca | athānenaiva vidhānena
                        kuṭajapalāśāśvakarṇapāribhadrakabibhītakāragvadhatilvakārkasnuhyapāmārgapāṭalānaktamālavṛṣakadalīcitrakapūtīkendravṛkṣāsphotāśvamārakasaptacchadāgnimanthaguñjāś
                        catasraś ca kośātakīḥ samūlaphalapatraśākhā dahet | tataḥ
                        kṣāradroṇam udakadroṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhir āloḍya mūtrair vā yathoktair
                        ekaviṃśatikṛtvaḥ parisrāvya mahati kaṭāhe śanair darvyāvaghaṭṭayan
                        vipacet | sa yadā bhavaty accho raktas tīkṣṇaḥ picchilaś ca
                        tamādāya mahati vastre parisrāvyetaraṃ vibhajya punar agnāv
                        adhiśrayet | tata eva cakṣārodakāt kuḍavamadhyardhaṃ vā'panayet |
                        tataḥ kaṭaśarkarābhasmaśarkarākṣīrapākaśaṅkhanābhīragnivarṇāḥ
                        kṛtvā+āyase pātre tasminn eva kṣārodake niṣicya piṣṭvā tenaiva
                        dvidroṇe 'ṣṭapalasaṃmitaṃ śaṅkhānābhyādīnāṃ pramāṇaṃ prativāpya
                        satatam aprmattaś cainam avaghaṭṭayan vipacet | sa yathā
                        nātisāndro nātidravaś ca bhavati tathā prayateta | athainam
                        āgatapākam avatāryānuguptam āyase kumbhe saṃvṛtamukhe nidadhyād
                        eṣa madhyamaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.25ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.25ab</label> atidagdhe

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.25cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.25cd</label> kriyāṃ
                        kuryād bhiṣak paś cācchālitaṇḍulakaṇḍanaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.26ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.26ab</label>
                        tindukītvakkapālair vā ghṛtamiśraiḥ pralepayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.26cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.26cd</label> vraṇaṃ
                        guḍūcīpatrair vā chādayed athavaudakaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.27ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.27ab</label> kriyāṃ ca
                        nikhilāṃ kuryād bhiṣak pittavisarpavat | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.27cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.27cd</label>
                        madhūcchiṣṭaṃ samadhukaṃ rodhraṃ sarjarasaṃ tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.28ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.28ab</label> mañjiṣṭhāṃ
                        cadanaṃ mūrvāṃ piṣṭvā sarpir vipācayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.28cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.28cd</label>
                        sarveṣāmagnidagdhānām etad ropaṇam uttamam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.29ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.29ab</label> snehadagdhe
                        kriyāṃ rūkṣāṃ viśeṣeṇāvacārayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.29cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.29cd</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
                        pravakṣyāmi dhūmopahatalakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.30ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.30ab</label> śvasiti
                        kṣauti cātyarthamatyādhamati kāsate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.30cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.30cd</label> cakṣuṣoḥ
                        paridāhaś ca rāgaś caivopajāyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.31ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.31ab</label> sadhūmakaṃ
                        niśvasiti ghreyamanyanna vetti ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.31cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.31cd</label> tathaiva ca
                        rasān sarvān śrutiś cāsyopahanyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.32ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.32ab</label>
                        tṛṣṇādāhajvarayutaḥ sīdatyatha ca mūrcchati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.32cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.32cd</label> dhūmopahata
                        ity evaṃ śṛṇu tasya cikitsitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.33ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.33ab</label>
                        sarpirikṣurasaṃ drākṣāṃ payo vā śarkarāmbu vā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.33cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.33cd</label> madhurāmlau
                        rasau vā'pi vamanāya pradāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.34ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.34ab</label> vamataḥ
                        koṣṭhaśuddhiḥ syāddhūmagandhaś ca naśyati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.34cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.34cd</label>
                        vidhinā'nena śāmyanti sadanakṣavathujvarāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.35ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.35ab</label>
                        dāhamūrcchātṛḍādhmānaśvāsakāsāś ca dāruṇāḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.35cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.35cd</label> madhurair
                        lavaṇāmlaiś ca kaṭukaiḥ kavalagrahaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.36ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.36ab</label>
                        samyaggṛhṇātīndriyārthān manaś cāsya prasīdati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.36cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.36cd</label>
                        śirovirecanaṃ cāsmai dadyādyogena śāstravit || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.37ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.37ab</label>
                        dṛṣṭirviśudhyate cāsya śirogrīvaṃ ca dehinaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.37cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.37cd</label> avidāhi
                        laghu snigdhamāhāraṃ cāsya kalpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.38ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.38ab</label>
                        uṣṇavātātapair dagdhe śītaḥ kāryo vidhiḥ sadā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.38cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.38cd</label>
                        śītavarṣānilair dagdhe snigdhamuṣṇaṃ ca śasyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.39ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.39ab</label>
                        tathā'titejasā dagdhe siddhirnāsti kathaṃcan | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.39cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.39cd</label>
                        indravajrāgnidaghe 'pi jīvati pratikārayet || </l>
                    <p ana="trailer">iti śrīsuśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne 'gnikarmavidhair
                        nāma dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>

                <div n="13" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <note>The vulgate text is here transcribed from the 1938 edition, not
                        the 1931 edition.</note>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.1"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.1</label> athāto
                        jalaukāvacāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.2"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.2</label> yathovāca
                        bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.3"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.3</label>
                            nṛpāḍhya<pc> </pc>bāla<pc> </pc>sthavira<pc
                            > </pc>bhīru<pc> </pc>durbala<pc> </pc>nārī<pc
                        > </pc>sukumārāṇām anugrahārthaṃ paramasukumāro 'yaṃ
                        śoṇitāvasecanopāyo 'bhihito jalaukasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.4"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.4</label> tatra
                        vātapittakaphaduṣṭaśoṇitaṃ yathāsaṃkhyaṃ śṛṅgajalaukālābubhir
                        avasecayet sarvāṇi sarvair vā (viśeṣas tu visrāvyaṃ
                        śṛṅgajalaukālābubhir gṛhṇīyāt) || </l>

                 
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.5"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.5ab</label> bhavanti cātra
                        ślokāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇaṃ samadhuraṃ snigdhaṃ gavāṃ śṛṅgaṃ prakīrtitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād vātopasṛṣṭe tu hitaṃ tad avasecane || </l>

     

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.6"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.6</label> śītādhivāsā
                        madhurā jalaukā vārisaṃbhavā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt pittopasṛṣṭe tu hitā sā tv avasecane || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.7"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.7</label> alābu kaṭukaṃ
                        rūkṣaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ ca parikīrtitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāc chleṣmopasṛṣṭe tu hitaṃ tad avasecane || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.8"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.8</label> tatra pracchite
                            tanu<pc> </pc>basti<pc> </pc>paṭalāvanaddhena śṛṅgeṇa śoṇitam
                        avasecayed ācūṣaṇāt sāntardīpayā 'lābvā | (jalāyukā vakṣyante) || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.9"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.9</label> jalam āsām āyur
                        iti jalāyukāḥ jalam āsām oka iti jalaukasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.10"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.10</label> tā dvādaśa
                        tāsāṃ saviṣāḥ ṣaṭ tāvatya eva nirviṣāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.11"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.11</label> tatra saviṣāḥ
                        kṛṣṇā karburā alagardā indrāyudhā sāmudrikā gocandanā ceti | tāsu
                        añjanacūrṇavarṇā pṛthuśirāḥ kṛṣṇā varmimatsyavad āyatā
                        chinnonnatakukṣiḥ karburā romaśā mahāpārśvā kṛṣṇamukhī alagardā
                        indrāyudhavad ūrdhvarājibhiś citritā indrāyudhā īṣadasitapītikā
                        vicitrapuṣpākṛticitrā sāmudrikāḥ govṛṣaṇavad adhobhāge
                        dvidhābhūtākṛtir aṇumukhī gocandaneti | tābhir daṣṭe puruṣe daṃśe
                        śvayathur atimātraṃ kaṇḍūrmūrcchā jvaro dāhaś chardir madaḥ
                        sadanam iti liṅgāni bhavanti | tatra mahāgadaḥ pānālepananasya
                        karmādiṣūpayojyaḥ | indrāyudhādaṣṭam asādhyam | ity etāḥ saviṣāḥ
                        sacikitsitā vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.12"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.12</label> atha nirviṣāḥ
                        kapilā piṅgalā śaṅkumukhī mūṣikā puṇḍarīkamukhī sāvarikā ceti |
                        tatra manaḥśilārañjitābhyām iva pārśvābhyāṃ pṛṣṭhe snigdhā
                        mudgavarṇā kapilā kiṃcidraktā vṛttakāyā piṅgalā ''śugā ca piṅgalā
                        yakṛdvarṇā śīghrapāyinī dīrghatīkṣṇamukhī śaṅkumukhīḥ
                        mūṣikākṛtivarṇā 'niṣṭagandhā ca mūṣikā mudgavarṇā
                        puṇḍarīkatulyavaktrā puṇḍarīkamukhī snigdhā padmapatravarṇā
                        'ṣṭādaśāṅgulapramāṇā sāvarikā sā ca paśvarthe ity etā aviṣā
                        vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.13"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.13</label> tāsāṃ
                            yavanapāṇḍyasahya<pc> </pc>pautanādīni kṣetrāṇi teṣu
                        mahāśarīrā balavatyaḥ śīghrapāyinyo mahāśanā nirviṣāś ca viśeṣeṇa
                        bhavanti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.14"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.14</label> tatra
                        saviṣamatsyakīṭadarduramūtrapurīṣakothajātāḥ kaluṣeṣv ambhaḥsu ca
                        saviṣāḥ
                        padmotpalanalinakumudasaugandhikakuvalayapuṇḍarīkaśaivalakothajātā
                        vimaleṣv ambhaḥsu ca nirviṣāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.15"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.15</label> bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣetreṣu vicaranty etāḥ salilāḍhyasugandhiṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         na ca saṃkīrṇacāriṇyo na ca paṅkeśayāḥ sukhāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.16"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.16</label> tāsāṃ grahaṇam
                        ārdracarmaṇā, anyair vā prayogair gṛhṇīyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.17"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.17</label> athaināṃ nave
                        mahati ghaṭe sarastaḍāgodakapaṅkam āvāpya nidadhyāt bhakṣyārthe
                        cāsām upaharec chaivalaṃ vallūram audakāṃś ca kandāṃś cūrṇīkṛtya
                        śayyārthaṃ tṛṇam audakāni ca patrāṇi tryahāt tryahāc cābhyo 'nyaj
                        jalaṃ bhakṣyaṃ ca dadyāt saptarātrāt saptarātrāc ca ghaṭam anyaṃ
                        saṃkrāmayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.18"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.18</label> bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthūlamadhyāḥ parikliṣṭāḥ pṛthvyo mandaviceṣṭitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         agrāhiṇyo 'lpapāyinyaḥ saviṣāś ca na pūjitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.19"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.19</label> atha jalauko
                        'vasekasādhyavyādhitam upaveśya saṃveśya vā virūkṣya cāsya tam
                        avakāśaṃ mṛdgomayacūrṇair yady arujaḥ syāt | gṛhītāś ca tāḥ
                            sarṣaparajanī<pc> </pc>kalkodaka<pc> </pc>pradigdha<pc
                        > </pc>gātrīḥ salilasarakamadhye muhūrtasthitā vigataklamā jñātvā
                        tābhī rogaṃ grāhayet | ślakṣṇaśuklārdrapicuprotāvacchannāṃ kṛtvā
                        mukham apāvṛṇuyāt agṛhṇantyai kṣīrabinduṃ śoṇitabinduṃ vā dadyāt,
                        śastrapadāni vā kurvīta yady evam api na gṛhṇīyāt tadā'nyāṃ
                        grāhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.20"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.20</label> yadā ca
                        niviśate 'śvakhuravad ānanaṃ kṛtvonnamya ca skandhaṃ tadā jānīyād
                        gṛhṇātīti gṛhṇantīṃ cārdravastrāvacchannāṃ kṛtvā dhārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.21"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.21</label> daṃśe
                            toda<pc> </pc>kaṇḍu<pc> </pc>prādur<pc> </pc>bhāvair jānīyāc
                        chuddham iyam ādatta iti śuddham ādadānām apanayet atha
                        śoṇitagandhena na muñcen mukham asyāḥ saindhavacūrṇenāvakiret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.22"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.22</label> atha patitāṃ
                            taṇḍula<pc> </pc>kaṇḍana<pc> </pc>pradigdhagātrīṃ
                        tailalavaṇābhyaktamukhīṃ vāmahastāṅguṣṭhāṅgulībhyāṃ gṛhītapucchāṃ
                        dakṣiṇahastāṅguṣṭhāṅgulibhyāṃ śanaiḥ śanair anulomam anumārjayed ā
                        mukhāt vāmayet tāvad yāvat samyagvāntaliṅgānīti | samyagvāntā
                            salilasarake<pc> </pc>nyastā bhoktukāmā satī caret | yā sīdatī
                        na ceṣṭate sā durvāntā tāṃ punaḥ samyag vāmayet | durvāntāyā
                        vyādhir asādhya indramado nāma bhavati | </l>
                   
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.22x"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.22y">atha suvāntāṃ pūrvavat sannidadhyāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.23"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.23</label> śoṇitasya
                        yogāyogān avekṣya śatadhautaghṛtābhyaṅgas tat picudhāraṇaṃ vāi
                        jalaukovraṇān madhunā 'vaghaṭṭayet śitābhir adbhiś pariṣecayed
                        badhnīta vā kaṣāyamadhurasnigdhaśītaiś ca pradehaiḥ pradihyād iti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.23x"/>
                    
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.24"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.24</label> bhavati cātra |
                        kṣetrāṇi grahaṇaṃ jātīḥ poṣaṇaṃ sāvacāraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         jalaukasāṃ ca yo vetti tat sādhyān sa jayed gadān || </l>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne jalaukāvacāraṇīyo
                        nāma trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>

                <div n="14" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.1</label> athātaḥ
                        śoṇitavarṇanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.2</label> yathovāca
                        bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.3</label> tatra
                        pāñcabhautikasya caturvidhasya ṣaḍrasasya
                        dvividhavīryasyāṣṭavidhāvīryasya vā'nekaguṇasyopayuktasyāhārasya
                        samyakpariṇatasya yas tejobhūtaḥ sāraḥ paramasūkṣmaḥ sa rasa ity
                        ucyate tasya ca hṛdayaṃ sthānaṃ sa hṛdayāc caturviṃśati dhamanīr
                        anupraviśyor dhvagā daśa daśa cādhogāminyaś catasraś ca tiryaggāḥ
                        kṛtsnaṃ śarīram aharahas tarpayati vardhayati dhārayati yāpayati
                        cādṛṣṭahetukena karmaṇā | tasya śarīram anusarato 'numānād gatir
                        upalakṣayitavyā kṣayavṛddhivaikṛtaiḥ | tasmin
                        sarvaśarīrāvayavadoṣadhātumalāśayānusāriṇi rase jijñāsā kim ayaṃ
                        saumyas taijasa iti | atrocyate sa khalu dravānusārī
                        snehanajīvanatarpaṇadhāraṇādibhir viśeṣaiḥ saumya ity avagamyate
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.4</label> sa khalv āpyo
                        raso yakṛtplīhānau prāpya rāgam upaiti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.5</label> bhavataś cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         rañjitās tejasā tv āpaḥ śarīrasthena dehinām |
                        <caesura/>
                         avyāpannāḥ prasannena raktam ity abhidhīyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.6</label> rasād eva striyā
                        raktaṃ rajaḥsaṃjñaṃ pravartate | tad varṣād dvyādaśād ūrdhvaṃ yāti
                        pañcāśataḥ kṣayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.7</label> ārtavaṃ śoṇitaṃ
                        tv āgneyaṃ agnīṣomīyatvād garbhasya || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.8</label> pāñcabhautikaṃ tv
                        apare jīvaraktam āhur ācāryāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.9</label> vesratā dravatā
                        rāgaḥ spandanaṃ laghutā tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhūmyādīnāṃ guṇā hyete dṛśyante cātra śoṇite || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.10</label> rasād raktaṃ
                        tato māṃsaṃ māṃsān medaḥ prajāyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         medaso 'sthi tato majjā majjñaḥ śukraṃ tu jāyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.11</label> tatraiṣāṃ (?
                        sarva ) dhātūnām annapānarasaḥ prīṇayitā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.12</label> rasajaṃ puruṣaṃ
                        vidyād rasaṃ rakṣet prayatnaḥ | annāt pānāc ca matimān ācārāc cāpy
                        atandritaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.13</label> tatra rasa
                        gatau dhātuḥ ahar ahar gacchatīty ato rasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.14</label> sa khalu trīṇi
                        trīṇi kalāsahasrāṇi pañcadaśa ca kalā ekaikasmin dhātāv
                        avatiṣṭhate evaṃ māsena rasaḥ śukrībhavati strīṇāṃ cārtavam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.15</label> bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         aṣṭādaśasahasrāṇi saṅkhyā hy asmin samuccaye |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalānāṃ navatiḥ proktā svatantraparatantrayoḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.16"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.16</label> sa
                        śabdārcirjalasantānavad aṇunā viśeṣeṇānudhāvaty evaṃ śarīraṃ
                        kevalam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.17</label> vājīkaraṇyas tv
                        oṣadhayaḥ svabalaguṇotkarṣād virecanavad upayuktāḥ śukraṃ
                        virecayanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.18</label> yathā hi
                        puṣpamukulastho gandho na śakyam ihāstīti vaktum atho
                        naivā(ā.naiva cā)stīti athavā'(? ca)sti satāṃ bhāvānām abhivyaktir

                        vivṛtapatrakeśare kālāntareṇābhivyaktiṃ gacchati evaṃ bālānām api

                        nārīṇām | (? rajasi copacīyamāne śanaiḥ śanaiḥ
                        stanagarbhāśayayonyabhivṛddhir bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.24cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.24cd</label> tadabhāvāc
                        ca śīryante śarīrāṇi śarīriṇām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.25"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.25</label> abhighātāt
                        kṣayāt kopāc chokādd hyānāc chramāt kṣudhaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.25ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.25ab</label> ojaḥ
                        saṃkṣīyate hy ebhyo dhātugrahaṇaniḥsṛtam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.25cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.25cd</label> tejaḥ
                        samīritaṃ tasmād visraṃsayate dehinaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.26-27"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.26-27</label> tasya
                        visraṃso vyāpat kṣaya iti liṅgāni vyāpannasya bhavanti
                        sandhiviśleṣo gātrāṇāṃ sadanaṃ doṣacyavanaṃ
                        kriyā'(O.kriyā)sannirodhaś ca visraṃse stabdhagurugātratā
                        vātaśopho varṇabhedo glānistandrā nidrā ca vyāpanne mūrcchā
                        māṃsakṣayo mohaḥ pralāpo maraṇam iti ca kṣaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.28"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.28</label> bhavanti cātra
                        | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.28ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.28ab</label> trayo doṣā
                        balasyoktā vyāpadvisraṃsanakṣayāḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.28cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.28cd</label>
                        viśleṣasādau gātrāṇāṃ doṣavisraṃsanaṃ śramaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.28ef"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.28ef</label> aprācuryaṃ
                        kriyānāṃ ca balavisraṃsalakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.29ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.29ab</label> gurutvaṃ
                        stabdhatā'ṇgeṣu glānirvarṇasya bhedanam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.29cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.29cd</label> tandrā
                        nidrā vātaśopho balavyāpadi lakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.30ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.30ab</label> mūrcchā
                        māṃsakṣāyo mohaḥ pralāpo 'jñānam eva ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.30cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.30cd</label> pūrvoktāni
                        ca liṅgāni maraṇaṃ ca balakṣaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.31"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.31</label> tatra visraṃse
                        vyāpanne ca kriyāviśeṣair aviruddhair balamāpyāyayet itaraṃ tu
                        mūḍhasaṃjñaṃ varjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.32ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.32ab</label>
                        doṣadhātumalakṣīṇo balakṣīṇi'pi vā naraḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.32cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.32cd</label>
                        svayonivardhanaṃ yattadannapānaṃ prakāṅkṣati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.33ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.33ab</label>
                        yadyadāhārajātaṃ tu kṣīṇaḥ prārthayate naraḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.33cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.33cd</label> tasya tasya
                        sa lābhe tu taṃ taṃ kṣayamapohati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.34ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.34ab</label> yasya
                        dhātukṣayādvāyuḥ saṃjñāṃ karma ca nāśayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.34cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.34cd</label> prakṣiṇaṃ
                        ca balaṃ yasya nāsu śakyaś cikitsitum || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.35"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.35</label> rasanimittam
                        eva sthaulyaṃ kārśyaṃ ca | tatra śleṣmalāhārasevino
                        'dhyaśanaśīlasyāvyāyāmino divāsvapnaratasya cāma evānnaraso
                        madhurataraś ca śarīramanukrāmannatisnehānmedo janayati
                        tadatisthaulyamāpādayati tamatisthūlaṃ
                        kṣudraśvāsapipāsākṣutsvapnasvedagātradaurgandhyakrathanagātrasādagadgadatvāni
                        kṣipramevāviśanti saukumāryānmedasaḥ sarvakriyāsvasamarthaḥ
                        kaphamedoniruddhamārgartvāccālpavyavāyo bhavati āvṛtamārgatvād eva
                        śeṣā dhātavo nāpyāyante 'tyarthamato 'lpaprāṇo bhavati
                        pramehapīḍakājvarabhagandaravidradhivātavikārāṇāmanyataṃ prāpya
                        pañcatvam upayāti sarva eva cāsya rogā balavanto
                        bhavantyāvṛtamārgatvāt srotasāṃ atas tasyotpattihetuṃ pariharet |
                        utpanne tu
                        śilājatuguggulugomūtratriphalāloharajorasāñjanamadhuyavamudgakoradūṣakaśyāmākoddālakādīnāṃ
                        virūkṣaṇacchedanīyānāṃ dravyāṇaṃ vidhivadupayogo vyāyāmo
                        lekhanabastyupayogaś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.36"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.36</label> tatra punar
                        vātalāhārasevino
                        'tivyāyāmavyavāyādhyayanabhayaśokadhyānarātrijāgaraṇapipāsākṣutkaṣāyālpāśanaprabhṛtibhir
                        upaśoṣito rasadhātuḥ śarīram ananukrāman nalpatvān na prīṇāti
                        tasmād atikārśyaṃ bhavati so 'tikṛśaḥ
                        kṣutpipāsāśītoṣṇavātavarṣabhārādāneṣv asahiṣṇur vātarogaprāyo
                        'lpaprāṇaś ca kriyāsu bhavati
                        śvāsakāsaśoṣaplīhodarāgnisādagulmaraktapittānām anyatamam āsādya
                        maraṇam upayāti sarva eva cāsya rogā balavanto bhavanty
                        alpaprāṇatvāt atas tasyotpattihetuṃ pariharet | utpanne tu
                        payasyāśvagandhāvidārigandhāśatāvarībalātibalānāgabalānāṃ
                        madhurāṇām anyāsaṃ cauṣadhīnām upayogaḥ
                        kṣīradadhighṛtamāṃsaśāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmānāṃ ca
                        divāsvapnabrahmacaryāvyāyāmabṛhaṇabastyupayogaś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.37"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.37</label> yaḥ punar
                        ubhayasādhāraṇāny āseveta tasyān narasaḥ śarīram anukrāman samān
                        dhātūn upacinoti samadhātutvān madhyaśarīro bhavati sarvakriyāsu
                        samarthaḥ kṣutpipāsāśītoṣṇavarṣātapasaho balavāṃś ca sa satatam
                        anupālayitavya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.38"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.38</label> bhavanti cātra
                        | </l>

                        atyantagarhitāv etau sadā sthūlakṛśau narau | </l>

                        madhyaśarīras tu kṛśaḥ sthūlāt tu pūjitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.39ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.39ab</label> doṣaḥ
                        prakupito dhātūn kṣapayaty ātmatejasā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.39cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.39cd</label> iddhaḥ
                        svatejasā vahnir ukhāgatam ivodakam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.40ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.40ab</label>
                        vailakṣaṇyāc charīrāṇām asthāyitvāt tathaiva ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.40cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.40cd</label>
                        doṣadhātumalānāṃ tu parimāṇaṃ na vidyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.41ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.41ab</label> eṣāṃ
                        samatvaṃ yac cāpi bhiṣagbhir avadhāryate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.41cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.41cd</label> na tat

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.42ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.42ab</label> doṣādīnāṃ
                        tv asamatām anumānena lakṣayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.42cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.42cd</label>
                        aprasannendriyaṃ vīkṣya puruṣaṃ kuśalo bhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.43ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.43ab</label> svasthasya
                        rakṣaṇaṃ kuryād asvasthasya tu buddhimān | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.43cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.43cd</label> kṣapayed
                        bṛṃhayec cāpi doṣadhātumalān bhiṣak | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.43ef"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.43ef</label> tāvad yāvad
                        arogaḥ syād etat sāmyasya lakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.44ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.44ab</label> samadoṣaḥ
