                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        pañcendriyārthavipratipattir nāma triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                </div>


                <div n="31" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> ekatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.1</label> athātaś
                        chāyāvipratipattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.2</label> yathovāca
                        bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.3ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.3ab</label> śyāvā
                        lohitikā nīlā pītikā vā'pi mānavam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.3cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.3cd</label> abhidravanti
                        yaṃ chāyāḥ sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.4ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.4ab</label> hrīr
                        apakramate yasya prabhādhṛtismṛtiśriyaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.4cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.4cd</label> akasmād yaṃ
                        bhajante vā sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.5ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.5ab</label>
                        yasyādharauṣṭhaḥ patitaḥ kṣiptaś cordhvaṃ tathottaraḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.5cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.5cd</label> ubhau vā
                        jāmbavābhāsau durlabhaṃ tasya jīvitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.6ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.6ab</label> āraktā daśanā
                        yasya śyāvā vā syuḥ patanti vā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.6cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.6cd</label>
                        khañjanapratimā vā'pi taṃ gatāyuṣam ādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.7ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.7ab</label> kṛṣṇā
                        stabdhā'valiptā vā jihvā śūnā ca yasya vai | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.7cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.7cd</label> karkaśā vā
                        bhavedyasya so 'cirād vijahāty asūn || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.8ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.8ab</label> kuṭilā
                        sphuṭitā vā'pi śuṣkā vā yasya nāsikā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.8cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.8cd</label> avasphūrjati
                        magnā vā na sa jīvati mānavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.9ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.9ab</label> saṃkṣipte
                        viṣame stabdhe rakte sraste ca locane | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.9cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.9cd</label> syātāṃ vā
                        prasrute yasya sa gatāyurnaro dhruvam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.10ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.10ab</label> keśāḥ
                        sīmantino yasya saṃkṣipte vinate bhruvau | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.10cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.10cd</label> lunanti
                        cākṣipakṣmāṇi so 'cirādyāti mṛtyave || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.11ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.11ab</label> nāharaty
                        annam āsyasthaṃ na dhārayati yaḥ śiraḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.11cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.11cd</label>
                        ekāgradṛṣṭir mūḍhātmā sadyaḥ prāṇān jahāti saḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.12ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.12ab</label> balavān
                        durbalo vā'pi saṃmohaṃ yo 'dhigacchati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.12cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.12cd</label>
                        utthāpyamāno bahuśastaṃ pakvaṃ bhiṣagādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.13ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.13ab</label> uttānaḥ
                        sarvadā śete pādau vikurute ca yaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.13cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.13cd</label>
                        viprasāraṇaśīlo vā na sa jīvati mānavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.14ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.14ab</label>
                        śītapādakarocchvāsaś chinnocchvāsaś ca yo bhavet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.14cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.14cd</label>
                        kākocchvāsaś ca yo martyas taṃ dhīraḥ parivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.15ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.15ab</label> nidrā na
                        chidyate yasya yo vā jāgarti sarvadā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.15cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.15cd</label> muhyed vā
                        vaktukāmaś ca pratyākhyeyaḥ sa jānatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.16ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.16ab</label>
                        uttarauṣṭhaṃ ca yo lihyād utkārāṃś ca karoti yaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.16cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.16cd</label> pretair vā
                        bhāṣate sārdhaṃ pretarūpaṃ tam ādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.17ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.17ab</label> svebhyaḥ
                        saromakūpebhyo yasya raktaṃ pravartate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.17cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.17cd</label>
                        puruṣasyāviṣārtasya sadyo jahyāt sa jīvitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.18ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.18ab</label> vātāṣṭhīlā
                        tu hṛdaye yasyor dhvam anuyāyinī | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.18cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.18cd</label>
                        rujā'nnavidveṣakarī sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.19ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.19ab</label>
                        ananyopadravakṛtaḥ śophaḥ pādasamutthitaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.19cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.19cd</label> puruṣaṃ
                        hanti nārīṃ tu mukhajo guhyajo dvayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.20ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.20ab</label> atisāro
                        jvaro hikkā chardiḥ śūnāṇḍameḍhratā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.20cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.20cd</label> śvāsinaḥ
                        kāsino vā'pi yasya taṃ kṣīṇam ādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.21ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.21ab</label> svedo dāhaś
                        ca balavān hikkā śvāsaś ca mānavam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.21cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.21cd</label> balavantam
                        api prāṇair viyuñjanti na saṃśayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.22ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.22ab</label> śyāvā jihvā
                        bhaved yasya savyaṃ cākṣi nimajjati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.22cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.22cd</label> mukhaṃ ca
                        jāyate pūti yasya taṃ parivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.23ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.23ab</label> vaktram
                        āpūryate 'śrubhiḥ svidyataś caraṇāv ubhau | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.23cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.23cd</label> cakṣuś
                        cākulatāṃ yāti yamarāṣṭraṃ gamiṣyataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.24ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.24ab</label> atimātraṃ
                        laghūni syur gātrāṇi gurukāṇi vā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.24cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.24cd</label> yasyākasmāt
                        sa vijñeyo gantā vaivasvatālayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.25ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.25ab</label>
                        paṅkamatsyavasātailaghṛtagandhāṃś ca ye narāḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.25cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.25cd</label>
                        mṛṣṭagandhāṃś ca ye vānti gantāras te yamālayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.26ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.26ab</label> yūkā
                        lalāṭam āyānti baliṃ nāśnanti vāyasāḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.26cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.26cd</label> yeṣāṃ vā'pi
                        ratir nāsti yātāras te yamālayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.27ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.27ab</label>
                        jvarātisāraśophāḥ syur yasyānyonyāvasādinaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.27cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.27cd</label>
                        prakṣīṇabalamāṃsasya nāsau śakyaś cikitsitum || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.28ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.28ab</label> kṣīṇasya
                        yasya kṣuttṛṣṇe hṛdyair miṣṭair hitais tathā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.28cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.28cd</label> na śāmyato
                        'nnapānaiś ca tasya mṛtyur upasthitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.29ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.29ab</label> pravāhikā
                        śiraḥśūlaṃ koṣṭhaśūlaṃ ca dāruṇam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.29cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.29cd</label> pipāsā
                        balahāniś ca tasya mṛtyur upasthitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.30ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.30ab</label>
                        viṣameṇopacāreṇa karmabhiś ca purākṛtaiḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.30cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.30cd</label> anityatvāc
                        ca jantūnāṃ jīvitaṃ nidhanaṃ vrajet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.31ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.31ab</label> pretā
                        bhūtāḥ piśācāś ca rakṣāṃsi vividhāni ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.31cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.31cd</label>
                        maraṇābhimukhaṃ nityam upasarpanti mānavam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.32ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.32ab</label> tāni
                        bheṣajavīryāṇi pratighnanti jighāṃsayā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.32cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.32cd</label> tasmān
                        moghāḥ kriyāḥ sarvā bhavanty eva gatāyuṣām || </l>
                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        chāyāvipratipattirnāmaikatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
